        <script>
        var $ = jQuery.noConflict();
        const lightSchemeIcon = document.querySelector('link#lightico');
        const darkSchemeIcon = document.querySelector('link#darkico');
        matcher = window.matchMedia('(prefers-color-scheme: dark)');
        matcher.addListener(onUpdate);
        onUpdate();


        function onUpdate() {
            if (matcher.matches) {
                lightSchemeIcon.remove();
                document.head.append(darkSchemeIcon);
            } else {
                document.head.append(lightSchemeIcon);
                darkSchemeIcon.remove();
            }
        }
    </script>

      <script>
      function initSlider($slider) {
        if ( $slider.length && $slider.find('img').length > 2 && !$slider.hasClass('slick-initialized')) {
          setTimeout(function() {
            $slider.slick({
              autoplay: true,
              arrows: false,
              dots: false,
              infinite: true,
              slidesToShow: 2,
              slidesToScroll: 1,
              autoplaySpeed: 0,
              speed: 8000,
              pauseOnHover: false,
              cssEase: 'linear'
            });
          }, 500);
        }
      }

      $(document).ready(function(){
        $('.post-inner:visible .post-logo.slider').each(function() {
          initSlider($(this));
        });

        $(document).on('mouseenter', '.post-wrapper', function() {
          $(this).find('.post-inner.display-on-hover .post-logo.slider').each(function(){
            initSlider($(this));
          });
        });
      });
      </script>

      <script>
      function initSlider($slider) {
        if ( $slider.length && $slider.find('img').length > 2 && !$slider.hasClass('slick-initialized')) {
          setTimeout(function() {
            $slider.slick({
              autoplay: true,
              arrows: false,
              dots: false,
              infinite: true,
              slidesToShow: 2,
              slidesToScroll: 1,
              autoplaySpeed: 0,
              speed: 8000,
              pauseOnHover: false,
              cssEase: 'linear'
            });
          }, 500);
        }
      }

      $(document).ready(function(){
        $('.post-inner:visible .post-logo.slider').each(function() {
          initSlider($(this));
        });

        $(document).on('mouseenter', '.post-wrapper', function() {
          $(this).find('.post-inner.display-on-hover .post-logo.slider').each(function(){
            initSlider($(this));
          });
        });
      });

                        <div class="pt-st-13 pb-st-13 pl-st-12 pr-st-12 cta-block v1 dark_blue">
                            <div class="cta-content">
                                                                    <h3>Ready to discover the power of Commerce Grid?</h3>
<p>Connect to the world’s first commerce SSP.</p>
                                                            </div>
                            <div class="button-content">
                                <a class='icon-thin-arrow-right has-arrow'   href='https://www.criteo.com/talk-to-an-expert/' ><button class='button pt-st-5 pb-st-5 pl-st-6 pr-st-6 button__secondary'><span>Contact Sales</span><span class='arrow-2023'></span></button></a>                            </div>

<style>.body-lc-regular-font{font-weight:400}.body-lc-medium-font{font-weight:500}.body-lc-semibold-font{font-weight:600}.bnw-filters{filter:grayscale(100) brightness(1) contrast(2);mix-blend-mode:multiply}.layout__faq_2025 .monetization-content{-ms-flex:1;flex:1}.layout__faq_2025 .caption{display:block;font-size:var(--eyebrow-one);color:#3d1ef8}.layout__faq_2025 .monetization-content h4{font-size:var(--headline-four);font-weight:500;line-height:1.2;color:#000;margin-bottom:0}.layout__faq_2025 .text-block{border-bottom:1px solid #ddd;position:relative;cursor:pointer}.layout__faq_2025 .text-block.active:after h4{transform:rotate(180deg)}.layout__faq_2025 .text-block h4{font-size:var(--body-four);font-weight:500;display:-ms-flexbox;display:flex;-ms-flex-pack:justify;justify-content:space-between;-ms-flex-align:center;align-items:center;padding-right:140px;color:#000}.layout__faq_2025 .text-block h4 .challenge-arrow{display:inline-block;width:24px;height:24px;margin-left:12px;transition:transform .2s;background:url(/wp-content/themes/criteo2017/img/arrow-down-2025.svg) 50% no-repeat;background-size:20px 20px;position:absolute;right:0}.layout__faq_2025 .text-block.active h4 .challenge-arrow{transform:rotate(180deg)}.layout__faq_2025 .faq-content{display:none;line-height:1.5;padding-right:45px}.layout__faq_2025 .text-block.active .faq-content{display:block}</style>
        <section id="sID-9" class="layout__faq_2025 mt-st-12 mb-st-12">
            <section class="container">
                <div class="row">
                    <div class="col-md-3">
                        <div class="monetization-content">
                                                            <span class="uppercase-labels caption mb-st-6">FAQ’s</span>
                                                                                        <h4>Got questions? We've got answers.</h4>
                                                    </div>
                    </div>
                    <div class="offset-md-2 col-md-7">
                        <div class="monetization-texts">
                                                                                                                                        <div class="text-block pb-st-7 pt-st-7">
                                            <h4 class="">What sets Criteo's Commerce SSP apart from other SSPs?  <span class="challenge-arrow"></span></h4>
                                                                                            <div class="faq-content pt-st-4">
                                                    <p>Commerce Grid is the only SSP built to seamlessly connect media owners with commerce advertising budgets at scale. With exclusive access to Criteo’s proprietary shopping intent signals, insights, and unique formats, we empower the entire ecosystem to drive meaningful commerce outcomes:</p>
<ul>
<li>Media Owners: Maximize revenue by monetizing first-party (1P) supply with Criteo&#8217;s demand and third-party (3P) DSPs. Build direct sales with Deals of 1P supply using Commerce Audiences, and package 1P audiences with 3P supply in Deals.</li>
<li>Agencies: Access curated supply with Criteo&#8217;s Commerce Audiences while seamlessly executing buys through existing DSP workflows.</li>
<li>Retailers: Expand the reach of first-party data by activating it across offsite inventory in supply packages.</li>
</ul>
                                                </div>
                                                                                    </div>
                                    

                                                                                                            <div class="text-block pb-st-7 pt-st-7">
                                            <h4 class="">What demand is available on Commerce Grid?  <span class="challenge-arrow"></span></h4>
                                                                                            <div class="faq-content pt-st-4">
                                                    <p>Commerce Grid connects publishers to programmatic demand from all top DSPs, along with preferred access to Criteo’s first-party demand covering over 17,000 advertisers.</p>
                                                </div>
                                                                                    </div>
                                    

                                                                                                            <div class="text-block pb-st-7 pt-st-7">
                                            <h4 class="">What media formats does Commerce Grid support? <span class="challenge-arrow"></span></h4>
                                                                                            <div class="faq-content pt-st-4">
                                                    <p>Display, Video, Native, In-App, and CTV.</p>
                                                </div>
                                                                                    </div>
                                    

                                                                                                            <div class="text-block pb-st-7 pt-st-7">
                                            <h4 class="">How do I connect with Commerce Grid? <span class="challenge-arrow"></span></h4>
                                                                                            <div class="faq-content pt-st-4">
                                                    <p>Media owners can take advantage of our standalone integration method or use existing header bidding wrappers to integrate directly into Commerce Grid. As part of this integration, media owners have direct access to the Commerce Grid user interface and reporting tools.</p>
                                                </div>
                                                                                    </div>
                                    

                                                                                                            <div class="text-block pb-st-7 pt-st-7">
                                            <h4 class="">What demand will this integration enable? <span class="challenge-arrow"></span></h4>
                                                                                            <div class="faq-content pt-st-4">
                                                    <p>Through a single integration, media owners unlock direct, unique commerce demand from 17,000+ brands, retailers, and agencies sitting behind Criteo’s Commerce Media Platform.</p>
<p>In addition to this direct demand, media owners also tap into premium demand from 60+ third party DSPs plugged directly into Commerce Grid.</p>
                                                </div>
                                                                                    </div>
                                    

                                                                                                            <div class="text-block pb-st-7 pt-st-7">
                                            <h4 class="">What does Criteo do to prevent fraud and protect user experiences? <span class="challenge-arrow"></span></h4>
                                                                                            <div class="faq-content pt-st-4">
                                                    <p>As one of only six TAG Platinum certified SSPs for fraud and brand safety, Commerce Grid enforces strict ad quality standards to ensure peace of mind. We also deploy third-party ad scanning tools to monitor and manage ad quality in real-time, ensuring your users always receive the best ad experience.</p>
                                                </div>
                                                                                    </div>
                                    

                                                                                                            <div class="text-block pb-st-7 pt-st-7">
                                            <h4 class="">How does Commerce Grid support yield insights and optimizations? <span class="challenge-arrow"></span></h4>
                                                                                            <div class="faq-content pt-st-4">
                                                    <p>Commerce Grid offers robust testing to value your audiences and maximize yield, in addition to flexible packaging tools to create new revenue opportunities.</p>
                                                </div>
                                                                                    </div>
                                    

                                                                                    </div>
                    </div>
            </section>
        </section>

<script>
    // modal video embed auto-play and auto-shut-up
    jQuery(document).ready(function() {

        var btn = jQuery('body').find('[data-toggle="modal"][data-type]'); // the button
        var target = jQuery(btn.data('target')); // modal div
        var src = btn.data('src');
        var type = btn.data('type'); // youtube or pardot
        var modalBody = target.find('.modal-body'); // modal body
        var iframe;

        btn.click(function() {
            //console.log('modal opened: create iframe for ' + type);
            iframe = modalBody.html('<iframe width="100%" height="450" frameborder="0" allowfullscreen></iframe>').children('iframe');

            if (type === 'pardot') {
                //console.log('iframe pardot');
                iframe.load(function() {
                    //console.log('iframe loaded');
                    iFrameResize(); // the secret sauce!
                });
                iframe.attr('src', src);
            } else { // youtube
                //console.log('iframe youtube');
                iframe.attr('src', src + '?autoplay=1&enablejsapi=1&rel=0'); // video URL in the button's data attr
                ytTracker.init(); // <-- Decorate all new videos on the page, from the 400-line monstrosity GTM
            }
        });

        target.on('hidden.bs.modal', function(e) {
            //console.log('modal closed: stripping the contents');
            modalBody.html('');
        });

    });
</script><script type="speculationrules">
